........................................................................................................................IFADAUTOS  ////// IFADAUTOS: Commencement of Cabin Manufacturing Units  ////// The Company has informed that the production of the Cabin Manufacturing units of the company commenced from December 31, 2020 located at IFAD Industrial Park, Dhamrai project, Dhaka, which was financed out of the Rights Share utilization schedule fund. The monthly production will be in a single shift up to 300 units, annual production will be in a single shift up to 3600 units and in full swing production 100% capacity up to 10,000 units per annum (approximately).  /////// 2021-01-03
........................................................................................................................BEXIMCO  ////// BEXIMCO: Share Purchase of Beximco Power Ltd (BexPower)  ////// (cont. news of BEXIMCO): BexPower holds 80% shares in Teesta Solar Limited (TSL) and Korotoa Solar Ltd. (KSL) who have entered into a Power Purchase Agreement (PPA) with BPDB and an Implementation Agreement with the Government of Bangladesh for supply of 200MW and 30MW solar generated electricity from solar electricity plants to be established in Gaibandha and Panchagarh respectively. The balance 20% shares in TSL and KSL are held by the respective technical Partners from China. (end)  /////// 2021-01-03
........................................................................................................................BEXIMCO  ////// BEXIMCO: Share Purchase of Beximco Power Ltd (BexPower)  ////// The Company has informed that Bangladesh Export Import Company Ltd (Beximco Ltd) has purchased 35 million shares of Beximco Power Ltd (BexPower) at par valued at BDT. 350 million from Beximco Holdings Ltd. With this purchase the number of Beximco Ltd.'s shares in BexPower has increased to 75 million shares which is 75% of the total issued shares of BexPower. The remaining 25% shares in BexPower is held by Mr. A S F Rahman, Mr. Salman F Rahman, Mr. Nazmul Hassan and Mr. O K Chowdhury. (cont.)  /////// 2021-01-03

........................................................................................................................REGL  ////// BSEC NEWS: Awareness Message for Investors  ////// (Continuation of BSEC News - Awareness Message for Investors) 3. Do not pay any heed to rumors at the time of trading shares; it may cause loss to you. Even spreading rumor is legally prohibited. (Ref.: SEC letter no. SEC/SRMIC/2010/726 dated November 23, 2010). (end)  /////// 2021-01-03
........................................................................................................................REGL  ////// BSEC NEWS: Awareness Message for Investors  ////// Investors are requested to consider the following facts at the time of making investment decision in the Capital Market: 1. Without acquiring proper knowledge, information and experience regarding different aspects and matters of Capital Market, one should not invest in the Capital Market. 2. The gain or loss, whichever comes from the investment, it belongs to you. So, well - thought of investment decision based on knowledge and fundamentals of the securities may be real assistance to you. (cont.)  /////// 2021-01-03
